Go through the new quests!
==========================





The Black Hand @ Stormhaven (Stormhaven: 6nw2n)
--------------------------------------------
 1  The Black Hand
    Get a Humblinischtroinken sausage from
    A hobbit mother (lvl 8)  @ Humblin, the Hobbit Hamlet. (6sw from entrance)
    (King's castle: 3ws, 6sw)
    transport Valheim: 8ene2n to get to Abbie, open irondoor east, east.
    Give Humblinischtroinken sausage to mort. get payroll (wages) and 
    give payroll to QM
    Note: Need to have joined quest before you give sausage to mort to be able to get wages.
    S/G?, 5-100
    Reward: rep
 
 2  Return of the Black Hand
    Kill Tomb raider (lvl 60) @ Kaltor. Get idol of many hands from Tomb raider
    (seen in the lower part of the area with the charred skeletons)
    give idol of many hands to QM
    Note: easy mob but need exp sized group to walk around in area,
    aggressive charred skeletons (good exp area though).
    Note: Need to get the kill with a joined character for idol to pop
    S/G?, 55-100, must have solved Black hand
    Reward: 1.5M xp, rep, 1.5M gold

Sir Kayodin @ Plains of the north (Ultima: 3nd3n2e)
--------------------------------------------
 3  No laughing matter
    Buy HUGE pretzel from shop in Valheim (w,n from obelisk) and give to
    Jester (Chuckles the Jester, lvl 33) @ Ultima (top floor of ultima)
    (Ultima: uw3sesuwsdesu5n2u2neneun3w4nu2n2e2u)
    Note: Only one HUGE pretz available in the shop per reboot
    Note: Shop opens 5am, closes around 5pm?
    S, 15-100
    Reward: 1M xp, rep?

Telanis the Dirge Singer @ Shadowdwell (Drow: 4n2d,n2enend4nuwnw3s2w, open door s, s2e)
--------------------------------------------
 1  The Portal
    Join the quest, walk to a place where you can examine something.
    Go to the portal (Shadowdwell, top of the tower in the Fortress XP area)
    and kill the Black Reaver for a large hooked battleaxe
    (transport drow,4n2d,3n4w3n4wn5wn, open gate,wn4w, open,wn,all up)
    and give the battleaxe to QM
    G, 50-100
    Reward: 500k xp, 2M gold, rep, 20qp, clay jar

Tonkar, the merchant @ Fishing Village/Sea Routes (6wnw from ship to NC)
--------------------------------------------
 1  Hook, line and sinker
    Kill A small leopard shark (lvl 25?) @ Ocean Floor for fishing hook.
    Give fishing hook to QM
    Note: The leopard shark is located in the lower (underwater) no-recall area.
    Note: Need to kill it with a joined char for the hook to pop.
    S/G?, 35-100
    Reward: 5k gold, rep

 2  Investigate the Dead
    Get to room @ The City Of Myrridon.
    From ship to OC walk 2nws, open trap, d2e 
    (2w4sw2s3ws, open trap, d2e from recall)
    S/G?, 1-100
    Reward: rep

Eivin the hunter @ Valheim (Valheim: 5s2wn)
--------------------------------------------
 1  If at first you don't succeed
    fetch some gray antlers and give to Eivin
    (exp area near stormhaven, with firbolgs, the antlers are on a reindeer)
    Note: low/bad poprate on some gray antlers but reindeers are easy to kill
    Note: some occasional aggros (worms) in the area.
    S, 55-100, MC
    Reward: ?

Tapio, the weathered hunter @ Hunting lodge (Stormhaven: s4wdw4sws2w3n) 
(room in Ashinara - Roads2)
(or eastish from the Oasis of Cohn Shar (Medjai Warriors))
--------------------------------------------
 1  Collector's item
    Fetch lizard egg from ground @ Shadowdwell.
    transport drow, 4n2d,3n4wnw, kill militia veteran (lvl 76-80) for key.
    open gate, 3wse, open cage, south.
    Note: might be 2 eggs in the room. Eggs are locateable
    Note: Deviir part (south/west tower) of shadowdwell have many aggressive mobs
    but nothing an exp sized group can't handle.
    S, 35-100
    Reward: 15 rep

 2  Released from the torment
    Kill a werewolf (Maurique).
    transport Valheim: 17sw5se7swnw4ses4enese2n, open wall w, w
    Kill Maurique (lvl 102 as werewolf, lvl 34-35 as human).
    Note: Maurique has about 138300 hp (about 46100 hp withered)
    Note: Maurique is not aggressive and has no memory.
    Note: Maurique turns into a werewolf around 10pm in game time.
    Note: Maurique turns into a man again 5am in game time.
    Note: Can't attack Maurique while he's a man
    Note: Need to get the killing blow with a joined character, all joined gets it completed
    G, 40-100, Must have solved Collector's item
    Reward: 2M xp, rep

 3  Jurrasic Heart!
    Fetch heart of a Carnotaurus (lvl 106-110) @ The Ancient Lands (8n from entrance)
    and bring to QM.
    Note: Carnotaurus hits VERY hard! (about 2k dmg/round of combat)
    Note: Carnotaurus has about 89608 hp
    Note: Carnotaurus vuln fire
    Note: Carnotaurus is not aggressive
    Note: Need to get the killing blow with a joined character, all joined gets it completed
    S/G?, 50-100
    Reward: ??

--------------------------------------------
 1  Monkey Business
    Fetch banana from ground @ Gnome Village (new Thalos: 2en2e4ne2nen2en 7en2es)
    and give to QM
    S, 0-100
    Reward: rep 5

 2  Monkey Tennis
    Kill Master Conjurer (lvl 60) @ Karandras (3sed from FS) for key that is
    in the bag Master Conjurer is carrying, unlock door north, north,
    kill The Chimpanzee Librarian (lvl 51) for a
    Powerful Banana (can be located) and give to QM in Ravens Point
    Note: Powerful Banana only pops on reboot or might pop when Librarian dies.
    S, 51-100, must have solved Monkey Business
    Reward: 1M xp, rep 10, banana milkshake (Potion, lvl 50 spell of miracle)

Baron duChesne @ The Village of Lost Souls (Kultheas: 4s2w3s2w2sdswdw2s2w2n, 4n2eue2n, open door, north, open door w, west)
--------------------------------------------
 1  A Rotten Heart
    kill The Necromancer (lvl 111-115) @ Village of Lost Souls 
    (Kultheas: 4s2w3s2w2sdswdw2s2w2n) for
    the rotting heart of the Necromancer (drops on ground after the Necromancer
    is killed, 1 character that has joined the quest need to be in the same
    room upon Necromancers death). Get the heart and walk back to QM and
    say witch
    wait for Baron to finish talking and then give the heart to baron.
    Note: the heart only pops if someone that has joined the quest is standing in
        the room upon death.
    Note: Need to be above level 61-65?+ to enter The Village of Lost Souls
        seems too scary with lvl 60 Ro/Ro atleast
    Note: the necromancer is a non solo mob even though the quest is a solo quest,
        need a big group.
    S, 50-100
    Reward: 10M exp, 10M gold, medal of glory (Treasure worth 5M gold), rep

Specials: Abbreviations and order of appearance:
h+1     = +1 hitroll
d-2     = -2 damroll
m+7     = +7 mana
hp+5    = +5 hp
str+1   = +1 strength
int-1   = -1 intelligence
wis-2   = -2 wisdom
con+1   = +1 constitution
dex+2   = +2 dexterity
mv+8    = +8 moves
li+2    = +2 light
save-3  = -3 spell save (negative save is good)
breath+1= +1 breath save
petri-2 = -2 petrification save
rod-2   = -2 rod save (=wand/staff save, I think)
para-4  = -4 paralysation save
AGE+5   = +5 age
Ag      = Anti-good
An      = Anti-neutral
Ae      = Anti-evil
Agn     = Anti-good, Anti-neutral
Age     = Anti-good, Anti-evil
Ane     = Anti-neutral, Anti-evil
DARK    = Item is dark
LIGHT   = Item is light
ARTIFACT= Lasts 7 reboots and is then destructed.
          Until then, no new artifact of that type will pop... Not really
carried = Carried in the inventory of the mob that loads it
nolocate= Can't be located by spells. All Well items are nolocate.
norent  = Can't be stored. Disappears at reboot
no-ident= Can't be identified.
POD     = Pop On Death (created when the mob dies)
(i)     = invisible
(c)     = nodrop (placed before item's name)
(C)     = noremove (placed before item's name)

Artifact Mob: Mob that has a chance of spawning with a special artifacts.
              Probably any mob of lvl 75 or higher.
              Artifacts are equipped on the mob, but no-locate.
              Mobs: King Rok Thunderhammer, Ancient Coral Snake, A Fire Giant,
                    An acolyte of Sarakesh, An Alliance counsellor, The Warden,
                    The Charred Skeleton, An Elite Daedroth Guard, The monster,
                    A drow warrior, The Great Soulcrusher, A bloodthirsty Warg,
                    A ghost of a decapitated woman, Guardian of the Abyss,
                    Will, A crone of the crescent moon, A Medjai Warrior,
		    A creepy monster


Items are sorted after:
1: Type     Wear locations as seen in "eq", then misc. stuff
2: Levels   Mage - Priest - Rogue - ...
3: Money
4: Weight   Heaviest items last
5: Name
Exception 1: Keys are sorted after area. Then after name.
Exception 2: Orbs are sorted after well level. Then after name.

ORBS:
Orbs are KTV-only. May have affects not shown on "stats". Pops on the ground
in The Well. When invoked, the orb is transformed into an aura, worn at
"surrounded by". Command: "invoke orb".
They are also sold by Halvdan in Karandras and shopkeepers in Milorai.
